function checkForDigitalData(callback){
    var interval = setInterval(function(e){
        var theElement = window.digitalData;
        if(theElement.length === 0 || theElement === null) return;
        callback();
        clearInterval(interval);
    }, 400);
}

function modifyDigitalData(data) {
    checkForDigitalData(function(){
        var digitalData = window.digitalData;
        digitalData.login = data.login;
        digitalData.page.loginStatus = data.page.loginStatus;
    });
}

function checkIfStoredAnalytics() {
    var localStorageAnalytics = localStorage.getItem('analyticsInfo');
    if (localStorageAnalytics) {
        modifyDigitalData(JSON.parse(localStorageAnalytics));
    }
}

if (_satellite.getVar('storageCheck')) {
    checkIfStoredAnalytics();
}

        var formattedMenuString = 'T|2|' + firstLevelDescription + '|' + (firstLevelPosition + 1) + '|' + secondLevelDescription + ' - ' + thirdLevelDescription + '|' + columnOrder + '' + (rowOrder < 10 ? '0' + rowOrder : rowOrder) + '|N/A|.';
        return formattedMenuString;

    },
    approvedTrackClick: function approvedTrackClick(menulink) {
        var isMenuLink = false;
        if (/(ThirdLevelItems|SecondLevelItems|ToggleThirdCategories|thirdLevelMenu)/.test(menulink.className) || menulink && menulink.parentElement && /secondLevelMenu__/.test(menulink.parentElement.className) || menulink.closest('.thirdLevelMenu__mobile')) {
            isMenuLink = true;
        }
        if (!isMenuLink)
            return;
        var finalCondition = false;
        finalCondition = isMenuLink;
        return finalCondition;
    },
    firstLevelDescription: function() {
        var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024;
        if (ui.isSLP()) {
            var menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('[class*="firstLevelMenu__"] li');
            menuItemsArr = [].slice.apply(menuItems);
            var a = menuItemsArr.find(function(element, i) {
                if (/active/.test(element.className)) {
                    return element;
                }
            });
            return windowW ? document.querySelector('.firstLevelMenu__title--active').textContent.trim() : a.textContent.trim();
        } else {
            return windowW ? document.querySelector("#mobile-item-".concat(ui.firstLevelPosition())).textContent.trim() : document.querySelector("#item-".concat(ui.firstLevelPosition())).textContent.trim();
        }
    },
    firstLevelPosition: function() {
        var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024;
        if (ui.isSLP()) {
            if (windowW) {
                var index = false;
                var menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('.firstLevelMenu__title');
                menuItemsArr = [].slice.apply(menuItems);
                menuItemsArr.map(function(element, i) {
                    if (/--active/.test(element.className)) {
                        index = i;
                    }
                });
                return index;
            } else {
                var index = false;
                var menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('[class*="firstLevelMenu__"] li');
                menuItemsArr = [].slice.apply(menuItems);
                menuItemsArr.map(function(element, i) {
                    if (/active/.test(element.className)) {
                        index = i;
                    }
                });
                return index;
            }
        } else {
            var index = false;
            var section = window.screen.width < 1024 ? document.querySelectorAll("section[class*='menuSection'] section") : document.querySelectorAll("section[class*='menuSection'] > div > section");
            section = Array.from(section);
            section.map(function(element, i) {
                if (/display/.test(element.className)) {
                    index = i;
                }
            });

            return index;
        }
    },
    secondLevelDescription: function(theParent) {
        var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024;

        if (ui.isSLP()) {
            if (windowW) {
                return theParent.closest('.secondLevelMenu__mobile').querySelector('a').textContent.trim()
            } else {
                return theParent.querySelector('.secondLevelMenu__title').textContent.trim();
            }

        } else {
            if (windowW) {
                return theParent.closest('[class*="SecondLevelItems_detailsElementsSmallDevice"]') ? theParent.closest('[class*="SecondLevelItems_detailsElementsSmallDevice"]').querySelector('a,p').textContent.trim() : theParent.closest('[class*=ThirdLevelItems_activeMobileThirdLevel]').previousSibling.querySelector('a,p').textContent.trim()
            } else {
                return theParent.querySelector('[class*="SecondLevelItems_submenuTitle"]').textContent.trim();

            }
        }
    },
    order: function order(el, type) {
        var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024;
        var order = false;
        var menuLink = el;
        var columnOrder = function() {
            if (ui.isSLP()) {
                return windowW ? menuLink.closest("[class*=firstLevelMenu__content]").parentElement.parentElement.querySelectorAll('.firstLevelMenu') : menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenuContainer"]').querySelectorAll('.secondLevelMenu__dekstop');
            } else {
                return windowW ? menuLink.closest("[class*=SecondLevelItems_displaySubMenuMobile]").parentElement.querySelectorAll("section") : menuLink.closest('[class*="SecondLevelItems_displaySubMenuDesktop"]').querySelectorAll('ul');
            }
        };
        columnOrder = [].slice.apply(columnOrder());
        if (windowW && type === "column") {
            if (ui.isSLP()) {
                var newMenuLink = menuLink.closest("[class*=firstLevelMenu__content]");
                var newMenuLinkArr = [].slice.apply(newMenuLink.querySelectorAll('.secondLevelMenu'));
                return newMenuLinkArr.indexOf(menuLink.closest('.secondLevelMenu'))
            } else {
                var subElementsMobile = menuLink.closest('[class*="SecondLevelItems_submenuElements"]');
                var subElementsArr = [].slice.apply(subElementsMobile.querySelectorAll('[class*="SecondLevelItems_detailsElementsSmallDevice"],[class*="ThirdLevelItems_desactiveMobileThirdLevel"],[class*="ThirdLevelItems_activeMobileThirdLevel"]'));
                var newMenuLink = menuLink.closest('[class*="SecondLevelItems_detailsElementsSmallDevice"],[class*="ThirdLevelItems_activeMobileThirdLevel"],[class*="ThirdLevelItems_desactiveMobileThirdLevel"]')

                return Math.ceil((subElementsArr.indexOf(newMenuLink) + 1) / 2) - 1;
            }

        }
        //desktop
        if (!windowW && type === "column") {
            if (ui.isSLP()) {
                return columnOrder.indexOf(menuLink.closest('.secondLevelMenu'));

            } else {
                return columnOrder.indexOf(menuLink.closest('ul'));

            }

        }
        //mobile
        if (windowW && type === "row") {
            if (ui.isSLP()) {
                if (menuLink.closest('.secondLevelMenu__title')) {
                    return 0;
                } else {
                    var thirdLevelContainer = menuLink.closest('.thirdLevelMenu__mobile');
                    var thirdLevelLinkArr = [].slice.apply(thirdLevelContainer.querySelectorAll('li'));
                    var clickedThirdLevel = menuLink.closest('li');
                    return thirdLevelLinkArr.indexOf(clickedThirdLevel) + 1;

                }

            } else {
                if (menuLink.closest('[class*=SecondLevelItems_detailsElementsSmallDevice]')) {
                    return 0;
                } else {
                    var thirdLevelContainer = menuLink.closest('[class*=ThirdLevelItems_activeMobileThirdLevel]');
                    var thirdLevelLinkArr = [].slice.apply(thirdLevelContainer.querySelectorAll('li'));
                    var clickedThirdLevel = menuLink.closest('li');
                    return thirdLevelLinkArr.indexOf(clickedThirdLevel) + 1;
                }

            }

        }

        if (!windowW && type === "row") {
            if (ui.isSLP()) {
                if (menuLink.closest('.secondLevelMenu__title')) {
                    return 0;
                } else {
                    var thirdLevelContainer = menuLink.closest('.thirdLevelMenu');
                    var thirdLevelLinkArr = [].slice.apply(thirdLevelContainer.querySelectorAll('li'));
                    var clickedThirdLevel = menuLink.closest('li');
                    return thirdLevelLinkArr.indexOf(clickedThirdLevel) + 1;

                }

            } else {
                if (menuLink.closest('[class*=SecondLevelItems_submenuTitleCon]')) {
                    return 0;
                } else {
                    var clickedThirdLevel = menuLink.closest('[class*="ThirdLevelItems_listElements"]');
                    var thirdLevelLinkArr = [].slice.apply(menuLink.closest('[class*="ThirdLevelItems_leafNodes"]').querySelectorAll('[class*="ThirdLevelItems_listElements"]'));
                    return thirdLevelLinkArr.indexOf(clickedThirdLevel) + 1;
                }
                return;
            }

        }
        var filterColum = function() {
            if (ui.isSLP()) {
                if (windowW) {
                    var a = columnOrder.find(function(el) {
                        if (el.querySelector('.secondLevelMenu__title--active')) {
                            return el.querySelector('.secondLevelMenu__title--active');
                        }
                    });
                    return [].slice.apply(a.querySelectorAll('.secondLevelMenu__mobile'));
                } else {
                    return columnOrder;
                }
            } else {
                return columnOrder;
            }
        };
        filterColum().map(function(el, i) {
            var rgx = el.textContent;

            var title = function() {
                if (ui.isSLP()) {
                    return el.innerText.split("\n", 1)[0];
                } else {
                    return el.textContent.substr(0, secondLevelDescription.length);
                }
            };

            var theParent = function() {
                if (windowW) {
                    return linkTo;
                } else {
                    if (menuLink.className.indexOf("thirdLevelMenu--link") > -1 || menuLink.className.indexOf("ThirdLevelItems_submenuElementLi") > -1) {
                        return ui.isSLP() ? menuLink.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement : menuLink.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement
                    } else {
                        return menuLink.parentElement.parentElement;
                    }
                }
            };
            var secondLevelDescription = ui.secondLevelDescription(theParent());

            if (title() === secondLevelDescription) {

                if (rgx.indexOf(menuLink.textContent.trim()) > -1) {
                    var indexColumn = i;
                    var thisSlpTitle = ui.isSLP() ? /__title/.test(menuLink.className) : /_submenuTitle/.test(menuLink.className);
                    if (thisSlpTitle) {
                        if (menuLink.textContent === el.querySelector('[class*="_submenuTitle"]').textContent) {
                            switch (type) {
                            case "column":
                                order = indexColumn;
                                break;
                            case "row":
                                order = /\<\/a>/.test(menuLink.outerHTML) ? indexColumn = 0 : indexColumn + 1;
                                break;
                            default:
                                console.log("not column or row");
                                break;
                            }
                        }
                    } else {
                        var isSLPListElement = ui.isSLP() ? el.querySelectorAll('li') : el.querySelectorAll("[class*=ThirdLevelItems_listElements]");
                        // var thirdLink = windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu__mobile"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=thirdLevelMenu') : isSLPListElement;
                        var thirdLink = function() {
                            if (ui.isSLP()) {
                                return windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="secondLevelMenu__mobile"] .secondLevelMenu__content').querySelectorAll('[class*=thirdLevelMenu') : isSLPListElement;
                            } else {
                                // return windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="SecondLevelItems_displaySubMenuMobile"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=ThirdLevelItems_activeMobileThirdLevel] li') : isSLPListElement;
                                return windowW ? menuLink.closest('[class*="activeMobileThirdLevel"]').querySelectorAll('[class*=ThirdLevelItems]') : isSLPListElement;
                            }
                        };
                        thirdLink = [].slice.apply(thirdLink());
                        thirdLink.map(function(el, i) {
                            if (el.textContent.trim() === menuLink.textContent.trim()) {
                                switch (type) {
                                case "column":
                                    order = indexColumn;
                                    break;
                                case "row":
                                    order = ui.isSLP() ? i - 1 : i + 1;
                                    break;
                                default:
                                    console.log("not column or row");
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }
                }
            }
        });
        return order;
    }
};

function addIsPLP() {
    //add isPLP desktop and mobile -
    var linksMenu = document.querySelectorAll('[class*="ThirdLevelItems_submenuElementLiBold"]');
    linksMenu.forEach(function (el, index) {
        el.href = el.href + '?isPLP=1';
    });
}
function addIsPLPexplorer() {
    var a = document.querySelectorAll('[class*="ThirdLevelItems_submenuElementLiBold"]');
    for (i = 0; i < a.length; i++) {
        a[i].href = a[i].href + '?isPLP=1';
    }

}
function isIE() {
    ua = navigator.userAgent;
    /* MSIE used to detect old browsers and Trident used to newer ones*/
    var is_ie = ua.indexOf("MSIE ") > -1 || ua.indexOf("Trident/") > -1;
    return is_ie;
}
function executeIsPLP() {
    /* Create an alert to show if the browser is IE or not */
    if (isIE()) {
        setTimeout(addIsPLPexplorer, 1000);
    } else {
        addIsPLP();
    }
}
executeIsPLP();

//setInterval(checkSkuBasket, 100);

function checkSkuBasket() {
    var counter = 0;
    document.querySelectorAll('.fb-basket__order-container__details > .fb-product-item').forEach(function(el) {
        counter = counter + 1;
    });

    if (counter > 0) {
        hideBuyButton(counter);
    }
}

function hideBuyButton(int) {
    var buyButton = document.querySelectorAll('.fb-order-status__continue-purchase');
    if (int > 10) {
        buyButton.forEach(function(el) {
            el.classList.add('fb-btn-disabled');
            el.classList.remove('fb-btn-primary');

            el.style.pointerEvents = "none";
            el.parentNode.style.cursor = "not-allowed";
            createTextOrderStatus();
        })
    } else {
        buyButton.forEach(function(el) {
            el.classList.remove('fb-btn-disabled');
            el.classList.add('fb-btn-primary');
            el.style.pointerEvents = "auto";
            el.parentNode.style.cursor = "pointer";
            deleteTextOrderStatus();
        })

    }
}

function createTextOrderStatus() {
    var orderStatusArray = document.querySelector('.fb-order-status');
    if (!orderStatusArray.querySelector('.disableText')) {
        var disableTextContainer=document.createElement('div');
        disableTextContainer.classList.add('cyberday-warning-basket-container');
        var disableText = document.createElement('div');
        disableText.classList.add('fb-order-status__sub-totals__copy');
        disableText.classList.add('disableText');
      //<i class="alert-icon-warning-ux"></i>
        disableText.innerHTML = '<i class="alert-icon-warning-ux"></i> Para asegurar la mejor experiencia coloca como m\u00E1ximo 10 productos en tu bolsa.\nSi tienes m\u00E1s productos col\u00F3calos en una nueva orden.';
        disableTextContainer.appendChild(disableText)
        orderStatusArray.appendChild(disableTextContainer);
    }

}

function deleteTextOrderStatus() {
    var orderStatusArray = document.querySelectorAll('.fb-order-status');
    orderStatusArray.forEach(function(el) {
        if (el.querySelector('.cyberday-warning-basket-container')) {
            el.querySelector('.cyberday-warning-basket-container').remove();
        }
    });
  
  

}

var api = {
    getAccengageCurrentDate: function(x){
        var hours = x.toString().match(/\d\d:\d\d:\d\d/);
        var day = x.getDate();
        var month = x.getMonth() + 1;
        var year = x.getFullYear();
        var string = year + '-' + month + '-' + day + ' ' + hours;
        return string;    
    }
}

      var interval = setInterval(function (e) {
        var theElement = document.getElementById(el) || document.querySelectorAll(el);
        if (theElement.length === 0 || theElement === null) return;
        callback();

      } else {

    }

      }

      return pageValid;
    }

        arrSecondlevelItems.map(function(el){

            //if(el.querySelector('.sale_ticket')) return;
            var thirdMenu = el.querySelectorAll('a[class*="thirdLevelMenu"]');

            var firstArrX = arrThirdMenu[0];
            var lastArrX = arrThirdMenu[arrThirdMenu.length -2]
            if(arrThirdMenu.length){
                arrThirdMenu.map(function(el){
                    var text = el.textContent.normalize('NFD').replace(/[^\w\s]/gi, '').toLowerCase();
                    if (/nuevo/.test(text) && firstArrX.textContent === el.textContent) {
                        if(text.length >= 22) return;

function fixArr(arr) {
    if (typeof (arr) === "object" && arr[0] && arr[0].skuId) {
        return arr;
    }

    if (typeof (arr) === undefined) {
        return null;
    }
    var temporalArr = [];
    if (Array.isArray(arr)) {
        temporalArr = arr;
    }
    if (typeof (arr) === "string") {
        temporalArr = arr.split(",");
    }

    var fixedArray = []
    temporalArr.forEach(function(el) {
        fixedArray.push({
            "skuId": el
        });
    });
    return fixedArray;

}

function fetchProductUpdatedInfo(skuString, callback) {

    //XMLHttpRequest
    var skuObj = fixArr(skuString);
    if (skuObj) {
        var fetchItemDetailRequest = new XMLHttpRequest();
        var fetchItemDetailURL = "/s/browse/v1/fetchItemDetails/co?" + encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify({
            "products": skuObj
        }));

        fetchItemDetailRequest.addEventListener('load', function(event) {

                var response = JSON.parse(this.responseText);
                if (response.success && response.success === true) {
                    var filteredProducts = response.products.map(function(el) {
                        if (el.product.published !== false && el.product.purchasable !== false) {

                            var tempEl = {};
                            tempEl.id = el.product.id;
                            tempEl.prices = el.product.prices;
                            tempEl.prices.forEach(function(el2) {
                                el2.price = el2.originalPrice||el2.formattedLowestPrice;
                                delete el2.originalPrice;
                                delete el2.label;
                                delete el2.isLoyalty;
                                delete el2.opportunidadUnica;
                                delete el2.symbol;

                            });
                            return tempEl;

                        }
                    });
                  if(callback){
                       callback(filteredProducts);
                  }else{
                    console.log(filteredProducts);
                  }


                }

                if (response.success && response.success === false && callback) {
                     callback(null);

                }
        });

        fetchItemDetailRequest.open("GET", fetchItemDetailURL, true);
        fetchItemDetailRequest.send();
    }
}

window.fetchProductUpdatedInfo=fetchProductUpdatedInfo;

<script>_satellite["_runScript25"](function(event, target, Promise) {
var pageName=_satellite.getVar('page_pageType')?_satellite.getVar('page_pageType'):_satellite.getVar('page_pageName');
switch (pageName) {
	case 'product detail page':
		syteDataLayer = window.syteDataLayer || [];
		syteDataLayer.push({

	default:
		syteDataLayer = window.syteDataLayer || [];
		syteDataLayer.push({
			name: 'fe_page_view',
			tag: 'ecommerce'
		});

		break;
}


function getProd() {

	var prodsArr = []
	digitalData.ecom.productList.forEach(function (el) {
		var tempObj = {
			'sku': el.sku,
			'price': el.price,
			'quantity': el.quantity
		};
		prodsArr.push(tempObj);
	});
	return prodsArr;
}

function getTotal() {
	var total = 0;
	digitalData.ecom.productList.forEach(function (el) {
		total = el.price + total;
	})
	return total;
}
